        <p data-mce-fragment="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;" data-mce-fragment="1" data-mce-style="font-weight: 400;">We aren’t sure who is louder: someone from Boston or a Yankees fan at a Red Sox game at the bottom of the ninth. </span></p>
<p data-mce-fragment="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;" data-mce-fragment="1" data-mce-style="font-weight: 400;">Show your New York pride with the Post’s jeering “Boston Sucks” tee, perfect to wear to the baseball game or just along the east coast to spark some heated debates in heavy accents. </span></p>
• 100% combed and ring-spun cotton (Heather colors contain polyester)<br> • Fabric weight: 4.2 oz./yd.² (142 g/m²)<br> • Pre-shrunk fabric<br> • Side-seamed construction<br> • Shoulder-to-shoulder taping<br> • Blank product sourced from Nicaragua, Mexico, Honduras, or the US<br> <br> This product is made especially for you as soon as you place an order, which is why it takes us a bit longer to deliver it to you. Making products on demand instead of in bulk helps reduce overproduction, so thank you for making thoughtful purchasing decisions!
